# Step 1: Merges the two datasets together
# Imports the fundamentals and market csvs
fundamentals_df = pd.read_csv('fundamentals.csv')
markets_df = pd.read_csv('market.csv')
# Merge dataframes
combined_df = pd.merge(fundamentals_df,markets_df,how='left', left_on=['FirmID','Year'], right_on = ['FirmID','Year'])
# Get information on dataframe
combined_df.info()

In [5]:
# Step 2: Creates six new variables to add to the dataframe (“CashRatio”, “DARatio”, “ROA”, “DivPayer”, “LnAssets” and “LnAge”)
# CashRatio = Cash / Assets
combined_df['CashRatio'] = combined_df['Cash']/combined_df['Assets']
# DARatio = LTDebt / Assets
combined_df['DARatio'] = combined_df['LTDebt']/combined_df['Assets']
# ROA = EBITDA / Assets
combined_df['ROA'] = combined_df['EBITDA']/combined_df['Assets']
# DivPayer = {1 if Dividends > 0, 0 Otherwise}
combined_df['DivPayer'] = (combined_df['Dividends'] > 0).astype(float)
# LnAssets=ln(Assets x 1,000,000) (Note: mt.log returns the natural logarithm is only one argument is passed into the function)
combined_df['LnAssets'] = np.log(combined_df['Assets']*1000000)
# LnAge = ln(Age) (Note: mt.log returns the natural logarithm is only one argument is passed into the function)
combined_df['LnAge'] = np.log(combined_df['Age'])
# Shows values for firm with FirmID 4115 in year 2005
firm_4115_2005_df = combined_df[(combined_df['FirmID'] == 4115) & (combined_df['Year'] == 2005)]
list_to_print = ['CashRatio', 'DARatio', 'ROA', 'DivPayer', 'LnAssets','LnAge']
for item in list_to_print:
    print(firm_4115_2005_df[item])

# Step 5: Carry out a t-test for the difference in means to test the null hypothesis.
# H0: There is no difference in the cash ratio between firms that pay a dividend and firms that don’t pay a dividend.
# Assume unequal variances between the two groups when carrying out the t test.

# SAS Implementation
# Sorts by Dividend Payer
sass_output = session.submit('''proc sort data=WORK._df;
by DivPayer;
run; ''',results = 'TEXT')

# Finds the means between the. two data groups
sass_output = session.submit('''proc means data=WORK._df noprint;
var CashRatio;
by DivPayer;
output out=MeansOutput;
run; ''',results = 'TEXT')

# Runs the ttest
sass_output = session.submit('''proc ttest data=MeansOutput;
class DivPayer;
var CashRatio;
run; ''',results = 'TEXT')
print(sass_output['LST'])

# Python implementation
# Create the data sets from the combined dataframe
pay_dividend_df = combined_df[(combined_df['DivPayer'] > 0)]
no_pay_dividend_df = combined_df[(combined_df['DivPayer'] == 0)]

# Calculates the difference in means (Expected to be 0.1013)
diff_means = abs(pay_dividend_df['CashRatio'].mean() - no_pay_dividend_df['CashRatio'].mean())

In [9]:
# Step 6: Produce a line chart that shows how the annual cash ratio varies over the sample period for firms as a whole. The chart should show two series:
# a. The equally weighted average cash ratio across all firms by year.
# b. The average cash ratio by year, value weighted across firms according to firms’ market capitalisation each year.

# Finds the unique number of years in the dataframe
years = sorted(combined_df['Year'].unique())

# Calculates the weighted average and for the years in the dataframe
weighted_ave = []
value_weighted_average = []
for year in years:
    # Creates dataframe for specific year
    loop_df = combined_df[(combined_df['Year'] == year)]
    # Creates the weighted average for this year
    weighted_ave.append(loop_df['CashRatio'].mean())
    # Calculates total market capitalisation for this year
    total_market_cap = loop_df['MarketCap'].sum()
    # Initialises value weighted average value
    value_weighted_average_value = 0
    # Uses for loop to calculate value weighted average for this year
    for index, row in loop_df.iterrows():
        value_weighted_average_value = value_weighted_average_value + ((row['MarketCap']/total_market_cap)*row['CashRatio'])
    # Append value to list for plotting
    value_weighted_average.append(value_weighted_average_value)

# Plots weighted average and value 
plt.plot(years,weighted_ave,'k',label = 'Equally Weighted')
plt.plot(years,value_weighted_average,'r',label = 'Value Weighted')
plt.xlabel('Year')
plt.ylabel('Cash Ratio')
plt.title('Cash Ratio Averages')
plt.legend()
plt.savefig("cash-ratio-averages.png")

# Step 7: Calculate LagReturn 
# Perform an initial shift
combined_df['LagReturn'] = (combined_df.sort_values(by=['Year'], ascending=True)
                       .groupby(['FirmID'])['Return'].shift(1))

# Checks the LagReturn variable for FirmID 5540 in Year 2002 (0.0446885931)
firm_5540_2002_df = combined_df[(combined_df['FirmID'] == 5540) & (combined_df['Year'] == 2002)]
list_to_print = ['LagReturn']
for item in list_to_print:
    print(firm_5540_2002_df[item])

In [11]:
# Perform corrections in LagReturns
# Groups via FirmID to get counting variables
grouped_df = combined_df.groupby('FirmID')
# Establishs counting variables
num_firms = 0
count = 0
total = 0
# Interates through the dataframe correcting for delisting and subsequent relisting
for key, item in grouped_df:
    # Groups via firm
    firm_df = grouped_df.get_group(key)
    # Creates list of dataframe index positions with the FirmID key
    firm_indexes = combined_df.index[combined_df['FirmID'] == key].tolist()
    # Iterates through each firms entry
    for x in range(len(firm_indexes)-1):
        # Checks for year increment irregularities which imply delisting and relisting (Take caution as uses chained indexing)
        if combined_df['Year'][firm_indexes[x+1]] - combined_df['Year'][firm_indexes[x]] > 1:
            combined_df.at[firm_indexes[x+1],'LagReturn'] = np.nan
            count = count + 1
    total = total + count
    count = 0
print(num_firms + total)

quit;
''',results = 'TEXT')

# Step 8.3: Fitting Linear Regressions
#  Multiple Independant Variables, a Dummy Variable and Industry Fixed Effects 
# (LnAssets, LnAge, DARatio, DivPayer, LagReturn, SIC Industry Fixed Effects vs Cash Ratio)
# Model: 𝐶𝑎𝑠ℎ𝑅𝑎𝑡𝑖𝑜𝑖,𝑡=𝛽0+𝛽1𝐿𝑛𝐴𝑠𝑠𝑒𝑡𝑠𝑖,𝑡+𝛽2𝐿𝑛𝐴𝑔𝑒𝑖,𝑡+𝛽3𝐷𝐴𝑅𝑎𝑡𝑖𝑜𝑖,𝑡+𝛽4𝐷𝑖𝑣𝑃𝑎𝑦𝑒𝑟𝑖,𝑡+𝛽5𝐿𝑎𝑔𝑅𝑒𝑡𝑢𝑟𝑛𝑖,𝑡+𝑆𝐼𝐶 𝐼𝑛𝑑𝑢𝑠𝑡𝑟𝑦 𝐺𝑟𝑜𝑢𝑝 𝐹𝑖𝑥𝑒𝑑 𝐸𝑓𝑓𝑒𝑐𝑡𝑠+𝜀𝑖,𝑡

sass_output = session.submit('''
title OLS regression: LnAssets, LnAge, DARatio, DivPayer, LagReturn, SIC Industry vs Cash Ratio;
proc glm data=WORK._df;
class SICIndustry;
model CashRatio = LnAssets LnAge DARatio DivPayer LagReturn SICIndustry / solution;
run; 
quit;
''',results = 'TEXT')
print(sass_output['LST'])

# Part II: Corporate Cash Holdings
# Creates new variables for the dataset
# ROE = EBITDA / Equity, ROENI = NetIncome / Equity, ROENI = NetIncome / Equity
combined_df['ROE'] = combined_df['EBITDA']/combined_df['Equity']
combined_df['ROANI'] = combined_df['NetIncome']/combined_df['Assets']
combined_df['ROENI'] = combined_df['NetIncome']/combined_df['Equity']

# Coverts dataframe to sas data for SAS Sessions
sass_dataset = session.dataframe2sasdata(combined_df)

# Produces summary statistics for the analysis
sass_output = session.submit('''proc means data=WORK._df stackodsoutput n mean std min p25 median p75 max;
var Assets Cash CurAssets EBITDA Equity NetIncome CashRatio ROA ROE ROANI ROENI;
run; ''',results = 'TEXT')
print(sass_output['LST'])

# Performs Time-series Analysis

# Finds the unique number of years in the dataframe
years = sorted(combined_df['Year'].unique())

# Initialises variable arrays
weighted_ave = []
value_weighted_average = []
roa_ni = []
roe_ni = [] 
assets = []
current_assets = []
cash = []
CARatio = []
for year in years:
    # Creates dataframe for specific year
    loop_df = combined_df[(combined_df['Year'] == year)]
    # Creates the weighted average for this year
    weighted_ave.append(loop_df['CashRatio'].mean())
    # Calculates total market capitalisation for this year
    total_market_cap = loop_df['MarketCap'].sum()
    # Calculate the mean ROA and ROE for this year
    roa_ni.append(loop_df['ROANI'].mean())
    roe_ni.append(loop_df['ROENI'].mean())
    # Appends total asset values to asset array and performs asset calculations
    assets.append(loop_df['Assets'].sum())
    current_assets.append(loop_df['CurAssets'].sum())
    cash.append(loop_df['Cash'].sum())
    CARatio.append((loop_df['CurAssets'].sum())/(loop_df['Assets'].sum()))
    # Initialises value weighted average value
    value_weighted_average_value = 0
    # Uses for loop to calculate value weighted average for this year
    for index, row in loop_df.iterrows():
        value_weighted_average_value = value_weighted_average_value + ((row['MarketCap']/total_market_cap)*row['CashRatio'])
    # Append value to list for plotting
    value_weighted_average.append(value_weighted_average_value)

# Plots weighted average and value CasRatio
plt.plot(years,weighted_ave,'k',label = 'Equally Weighted')
plt.plot(years,value_weighted_average,'r',label = 'Value Weighted')
plt.xlabel('Year')
plt.ylabel('Cash Ratio')
plt.title('Cash Ratio Averages')
plt.legend()
plt.savefig("cash-ratio-averages.png")
plt.clf()

# Plot returns over time
plt.xlim(1950, 2020)
plt.ylim(-0.5,0.5)
plt.plot(years,roa_ni,'g',label = 'ROA (Net Income)')
plt.xlabel('Year')
plt.ylabel('ROA')
plt.title('ROA vs Years')
plt.legend()
plt.savefig("returns.png")
plt.clf()

# Plot the trends in assets
plt.plot(years,assets,'g',label = 'Assets)')
plt.plot(years,current_assets,'b',label = 'Current Assets')
plt.plot(years,cash,'r',label = 'Cash')
plt.xlabel('Year')
plt.ylabel('Returns')
plt.title('Assets vs Years')
plt.legend()
plt.savefig("assets.png")
plt.clf()

# Plots CashRatio overlayed with ROA
fig, ax1 = plt.subplots()
ax1.plot(years,weighted_ave,'k',label = 'Equally Weighted')
ax1.plot(years,value_weighted_average,'r',label = 'Value Weighted')
ax1.set_xlabel('Years')
# Make the y-axis label, ticks and tick labels match the line color.
ax1.set_ylabel('CashRatio', color='k')
ax1.tick_params('y', colors='k')
ax2 = ax1.twinx()
ax2.plot(years,roa_ni,'g',label = 'ROA (Net Income)')
ax2.set_ylabel('ROA', color='k')
ax2.tick_params('y', colors='k')
fig.tight_layout()
plt.title('CashRatio & ROA vs years')
plt.legend()
plt.savefig("cashratio-ROA.png")
plt.clf()
